 function gutterOver(num) {=0A=
 gutterOut();=0A=
 var newTR =3D document.getElementById('gr_svnNone_' + num);=0A=
 if (newTR) {=0A=
 newTR.className =3D 'undermouse';=0A=
 }=0A=
 lineNumUnderMouse =3D num;=0A=
 }=0A=
 function gutterOut() {=0A=
 if (lineNumUnderMouse !=3D -1) {=0A=
 var oldTR =3D document.getElementById(=0A=
 'gr_svnNone_' + lineNumUnderMouse);=0A=
 if (oldTR) {=0A=
 oldTR.className =3D '';=0A=
 }=0A=
 lineNumUnderMouse =3D -1;=0A=
 }=0A=
 }=0A=
 var numsGenState =3D {table_base_id: 'nums_table_'};=0A=
 var srcGenState =3D {table_base_id: 'src_table_'};=0A=
 var alignerRunning =3D false;=0A=
 var startOver =3D false;=0A=
 function setLineNumberHeights() {=0A=
 if (alignerRunning) {=0A=
 startOver =3D true;=0A=
 return;=0A=
 }=0A=
 numsGenState.chunk_id =3D 0;=0A=
 numsGenState.table =3D document.getElementById('nums_table_0');=0A=
 numsGenState.row_num =3D 0;=0A=
 srcGenState.chunk_id =3D 0;=0A=
 srcGenState.table =3D document.getElementById('src_table_0');=0A=
 srcGenState.row_num =3D 0;=0A=
 alignerRunning =3D true;=0A=
 continueToSetLineNumberHeights();=0A=
 }=0A=
 function rowGenerator(genState) {=0A=
 if (genState.row_num < genState.table.rows.length) {=0A=
 var currentRow =3D genState.table.rows[genState.row_num];=0A=
 genState.row_num++;=0A=
 return currentRow;=0A=
 }=0A=
 var newTable =3D document.getElementById(=0A=
 genState.table_base_id + (genState.chunk_id + 1));=0A=
 if (newTable) {=0A=
 genState.chunk_id++;=0A=
 genState.row_num =3D 0;=0A=
 genState.table =3D newTable;=0A=
 return genState.table.rows[0];=0A=
 }=0A=
 return null;=0A=
 }=0A=
 var MAX_ROWS_PER_PASS =3D 1000;=0A=
 function continueToSetLineNumberHeights() {=0A=
 var rowsInThisPass =3D 0;=0A=
 var numRow =3D 1;=0A=
 var srcRow =3D 1;=0A=
 while (numRow && srcRow && rowsInThisPass < MAX_ROWS_PER_PASS) {=0A=
 numRow =3D rowGenerator(numsGenState);=0A=
 srcRow =3D rowGenerator(srcGenState);=0A=
 rowsInThisPass++;=0A=
 if (numRow && srcRow) {=0A=
 if (numRow.offsetHeight !=3D srcRow.offsetHeight) {=0A=
 numRow.firstChild.style.height =3D srcRow.offsetHeight + 'px';=0A=
 }=0A=
 }=0A=
 }=0A=
 if (rowsInThisPass >=3D MAX_ROWS_PER_PASS) {=0A=
 setTimeout(continueToSetLineNumberHeights, 10);=0A=
 } else {=0A=
 alignerRunning =3D false;=0A=
 if (startOver) {=0A=
 startOver =3D false;=0A=
 setTimeout(setLineNumberHeights, 500);=0A=
 }=0A=
 }=0A=
 }=0A=
 // Do 2 complete passes, because there can be races=0A=
 // between this code and prettify.=0A=
 startOver =3D true;=0A=
 setTimeout(setLineNumberHeights, 250);=0A=
 window.onresize =3D setLineNumberHeights;=0A=
</SCRIPT>
</DIV>

ipts.js"></SCRIPT>
